***ik.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> (2)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ic</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:ek.html>ek</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*éǵh₂</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ich</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">I</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">jeg</i>.
See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">I</i> (English, etymology 3).<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:imbeciel.html>imbeciel</a> (8035)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">imbécile</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:imbeciel.html>imbeciel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:imbeciel.html>imbecieler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">imbecielst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">stupid</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">idiotic</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> now offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mentally <span class="Latn" lang="en">retarded</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">imbecilic</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">idiotic</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">mentally disabled with the mental age of a young child</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>1974</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:willem.html>Willem</a> Wilmink, "Frekie".
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:imbeciel.html>imbeciele</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jongen</a>. / <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mongool.html>mongool</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> an <b>imbecile</b> boy. / A retard.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:imbeciel.html>imbeciel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:imbecielen.html>imbecielen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:imbeciel.html>imbecieltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> now offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">imbecile</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">idiot</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">retard</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">mentally disabled person with the mental age of a young child</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">imbecile</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">idiot</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">dumbass</span></li></ol>

***immers.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:immers.html>immers</a> (5841)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:immer.html>immer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">always, ever</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">adverb-forming <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:immers.html>immers</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Indicates that an explanation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> being given for an earlier statement.</span>; indeed, after all
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:immers.html>immers</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevraagd.html>gevraagd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>No, he's already home, <b>because</b> he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> asked to come home.</dd></dl></li>
<li>“<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Bataven" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Bataven">Bataven</a>” on the Dutch Wikipedia:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:tijdens.html>Tijdens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Nederlandse <a href = vnd.unilang:opstand.html>Opstand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Spaanse <a href = vnd.unilang:overheersing.html>overheersing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschouwden.html>beschouwden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Nederlanders <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:nakomelingen.html>nakomelingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Bataven', <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:immers.html>immers</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:onderdrukker.html>onderdrukkers</a>', <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Romeinen, in <a href = vnd.unilang:opstand.html>opstand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gekomen.html>gekomen</a>.
<dl><dd>During and after the Dutch Revolt against the Spanish domination, the Dutch regarded themselves as the 'descendants of the Batavians', <b>for</b> they <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> [<i>literally</i> who <b><a href = vnd.unilang:immers.html>immers</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a>] also come to rebel against their 'oppressors', the Romans.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***immigratie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:immigratie.html>immigratie</a> (16098)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:immigreren.html>immigreren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-atie</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:immigratie.html>immigratie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:immigraties.html>immigraties</a></b>)

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blik.html>blik</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">can, metal, container</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blik.html>blik</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">glance, view</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>, or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blikken.html>blikken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to glance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***inboorling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:inboorling.html>inboorling</a> (32577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">inboorlinc</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geboren.html>geboren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ling</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inboorling.html>inboorling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inboorlingen.html>inboorlingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inboorling.html>inboorlingetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">inboorlinge</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A native, an aboriginal <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">member of the original population of a locale</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A native, one born in a certain place or region, especially a natively born resident.</li></ol>
